powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(18, 17, 17);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><strong>今日发音练习重点：</strong></span></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><strong>1. gr</strong></span><span style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><strong>ie</strong></span><span style="font-size: 14px;"><strong>f包含长元音、紧元音/i:/；</strong></span></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><strong>2. 注意区分n<span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);">a</span>tural<span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;text-align: start;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">/ˈn</span><span start;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">tʃrəl/</span>和n<span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);">a</span>ture/<span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;text-align: start;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">ˈn</span><span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);font-family: Arial, sans-serif;text-align: start;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">eɪ</span><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;text-align: start;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">tʃə(r)/</span>的发音。</strong></span><span style="font-size: 14px;"></span></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);text-align: left;margin: 20px 0% 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 40%;border-width: 0px 6px 0px 0px;border-style: solid;border-left-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);border-right-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);padding: 0px;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;background-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(252, 252, 252);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">言之有物</em></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. 词链儿：a natural part of life 生活中很自然的一部分</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Everyone gets angry sometimes, it's <em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">a natural part of life</span></strong></em>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">每个人都有生气的时候，这是<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">日常生活的一部分</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Disappointment is <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">a natural part of life</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">失望是<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">人生必不可少的一部分</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. 词链儿：go through tough grief 经历悲痛</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">*go through的三种常见用法：<br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-family: Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 13px;text-align: start;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">①</span>穿过</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Once you <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">go through</span></em></strong> this corridor, turn right.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="font-size: 14px;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-family: Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 13px;text-align: start;">②</span></strong>仔细查阅</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We need to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">go through</span></em></strong> these files</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="font-size: 14px;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_gif/yBE8wVymmQmMXgaNMcvPNibaHjul6icY1uia8owQJUGdvzeNh2Ejuda8K1ojdzWCeID36sV4pqicTgttUTT4UUHsqA/640?wx_fmt=gif" data-type="gif" data-w="640" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: -40px 0% 10px;text-align: center;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;margin-top: -10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;border-right-width: 8px;border-right-style: solid;border-right-color: rgb(185, 167, 121);border-bottom-width: 8px;border-bottom-style: solid;border-bottom-color: rgb(185, 167, 121);border-top-width: 8px !important;border-top-style: solid !important;border-top-color: transparent !important;border-left-width: 8px !important;border-left-style: solid !important;border-left-color: transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></section><section style="width: 0px;margin-top: -12px;margin-left: 4px;border-right-width: 5px;border-right-style: solid;border-right-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);border-bottom-width: 6px;border-bottom-style: solid;border-bottom-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);border-top-width: 6px !important;border-top-style: solid !important;border-top-color: transparent !important;border-left-width: 5px !important;border-left-style: solid !important;border-left-color: transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(114, 114, 114);border-bottom-right-radius: 0px;padding: 0px 5px 4px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词汇补充</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-top: 1.2em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-left: 0.7em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.7em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;line-height: 1.2;padding-left: 3px;padding-right: 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Vocabulary</strong></p></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgba(94, 169, 210, 0.6);padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">clear sth away</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：to make a place tidy by removing things from it or putting them where they should be清除；清理；整理</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I want you to clear all these toys away before bedtime.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我要你在睡觉前把所有的玩具都收拾好。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">go out</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：to leave a room or building, especially in order to do something for entertainment（尤指为了去娱乐）外出，出门参加社交活动</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Please close the door as you go out.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你出去玩的时候请把门关上。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：to have a romantic and usually sexual relationship with someone（与某人）谈恋爱（通常有性关系）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">How long have you been going out with him?</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你跟他恋爱有多长时间了？</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：If the tide goes out, it moves back and covers less of the beach.退潮，落潮</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：If a light or something that is burning goes out, it stops producing</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">light or heat.熄灭</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">When I woke up the fire had gone out.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">当我醒来时，火已经熄了。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：to lose when you are playing in a sports competition, so that you must stop playing in the competition（在比赛中）被淘汰，出局</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">England went out to France in the second round of the championship.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">锦标赛第二轮比赛中英格兰队被法国队淘汰出局。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">depend on/upon sb/sth</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：to trust someone or something and know that that person or thing will help you or do what you want or expect him, her, or it to do信任…，相信…</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You can always depend on Michael in a crisis.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">危机时刻你总是可以相信迈克尔。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：to need something, or need the help and support of someone or something, in order to live or continue as before需要；依赖，依靠</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Charities depend on people supporting their activities.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">慈善机构依靠民众支持他们的活动。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">have no time for sb</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：to disapprove of someone and not want to be involved with them对（某人）没好感，讨厌（某人）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I have no time for people who are always complaining.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我不喜欢老是抱怨的人。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">be no picnic</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：to be a difficult or unpleasant situation不是轻松愉快的事</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Being a single parent is no picnic, I can tell you.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我跟你说，做个单亲父母决非易事。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;padding: 0px 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;margin-top: 1.15em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 6px;height: 6px;margin-top: -3px;border-radius: 100%;float: left;background-color: rgb(232, 181, 181);box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style="border-top: 1px solid rgb(232, 181, 181);width: 99.9%;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section style="text-align: right;margin: -1.1em 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: border-box;">第三步   认真校对，查缺补漏</p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px;padding-left: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">听写方法：</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">完成今天的任务了么？不！千万不要丢掉极其重要的一步：校对！</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有两个方面要校对：</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.没有听出来的意群：可能包括连读或者省音,分析错误的原因并做笔记。</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.没有听出来或听错的单词:每篇校对后写在听写笔记下面并罗列,这些才是你每天的进步之基。</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">THE Lion was pacing to and fro about that empty land and singing his new song. It was softer and more lilting than the song by which he had called up the stars and the sun; a gentle, rippling music. And as he walked and sang the valley grew green with grass. It spread out from the Lion like a pool. It ran up the sides of the little hills like a wave. In a few minutes it was creeping up the lower slopes of the distant mountains, making that young world every moment softer. The light wind could now be heard ruffling the grass. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">狮子唱着新歌，在空旷的大地上走来走去。这歌声比刚才唤起星星和太阳的歌声更柔和，更轻快活泼，是一曲如潺潺流水般温暖的乐声。随着它的移动和歌唱，河谷里长出青青碧草，从狮子身边像水潭一样蔓延开去，又如浪花一般爬到小山坡上。一会儿，青草就长上了远处大山的斜坡，年轻的世界每一瞬间都变得更加柔美。徽风沙沙地拂动青草。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 在这个工程中你做的很好。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 谢谢你。这工作不容易，但是我高兴我能做到了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 恭喜你啊。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 那你什么时候给我加薪啊？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 这个嘛，我不确定。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 突然要求涨工资，实在不好意思。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 让我想想，那你想要加多少？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 每月5000元。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 那很多，让我仔细考虑一下。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: You did an excellent job in this project.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Thank you. It was a lot of hard work, but I'm glad I did it.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Congratulations.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: When will you give me a raise?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Hum… I'm not sure.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: I feel quite embarrassed for having to request a pay raise so quickly.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Let me think. How much do you have in mind?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 5000 Yuan per month.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: That's a lot of money. Let me think about it carefully.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">My waitress whipped the plate away and ____________ my bill.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我的服务员麻利地撤走盘子并搁下我的账单。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(18, 17, 17);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">今日发音练习重点：</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong>1. old<strong style="color: rgb(18, 17, 17);font-size: 14px;text-align: left;white-space: 255);">、</strong>control 包含易错音组/əʊl $ oʊl/；</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong>2. <strong style="color: rgb(18, 17, 17);font-size: 14px;text-align: left;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">注意</strong>gifts、fists、list的元音均为/ɪ/；</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong>3. myths /mɪθs/，其中/<strong style="color: rgb(18, 17, 17);font-size: 14px;text-align: left;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">θ</strong>/要求舌尖略伸出口腔，摩擦上齿。</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, border-box;">言之有物</em></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. 词链儿：the symbolic meaning of XX</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">XX的象征意义</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">symbol noun. 象征</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">symbolic adj. 象征的</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">symbolize verb. 象征着</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">symbolism noun. 象征主义</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. 词链儿：remain unchanged 保持不变</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">remain+adj. 保持adj. 的状态</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">3. long for reunion 渴望团聚</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链儿：long for XX 渴望XX</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">近义词：desire / crave / yearn</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">After years of war, the people <em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">long for</span></strong></em><g style="box-sizing: border-box;">a lasting peace</g>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">历经多年战乱之后，人民<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">渴望</strong>永久和平。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">longed for</span></em></strong> the good old days.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">渴望</strong>旧日归来。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">→longed-for adj. 渴望已久的</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">This is a <g style="box-sizing: border-box;">much </g><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><g style="box-sizing: border-box;">longed-for</g></span></em></strong> holiday for children.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对于孩子们来说这是一次<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">渴望已久的</strong>假期。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>I crave it, I <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">long for</span></em></strong> it.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我渴望它，我<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">渴望</strong>它。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>I started to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">long for</span></em></strong> nature again.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我又开始<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">向往</strong>大自然了。</p><p 0px 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="display: inline;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: unset;color: rgb(56, 56, 56);box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">If Nate wanted to<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"> turn us in</span>, he would have done it that night.</span></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">如果内特想要<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">抓我们</span>，他那晚就可以这么做。</span></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">If he hurts anyone else, I'll <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">turn us all in</span>.</span></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;">如果他伤害了任何人，我就</span><span style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">把事情都说出去。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">for God's sake</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">用于加强说话人的语气</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">意思可理解为“天啊；拜托”</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">“行行好吧；看在上帝份上”</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" could get the chair.</strong></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="display: inline;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">For God’s sake, </span><span style="font-size: 14px;">let's not make 'em again</span>.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">拜托 </span><span style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;">，</span><span style="font-size: 14px;">我们不要再犯同样的错了</span>。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">For God‘s sake </span><span style="font-size: 14px;">will you take those off</span>?</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">行行好吧</span>，<span style="font-size: 14px;">摘掉你的太阳镜</span>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 13px;color: rgb(104, 104, 104);line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 1px;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">公众号｜TeacherGwen</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">早读|口语|阅读|翻译|听写</p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Soon there were other things besides grass. The higher slopes grew dark with heather. Patches of rougher and more bristling green appeared in the valley. Digory did not know what they were until one began coming up quite close to him. It was a little, spiky thing that threw out dozens of arms and covered these arms with green and grew larger at the rate of about an inch every two seconds. There were dozens of these things all round him now. When they were nearly as tall as himself he saw what they were. "Trees!" he exclaimed.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">很快，除了草，又出现了别的东西。高高的山坡上长出了颜色暗淡的石南属植物，河谷里旨出了一片片毛茬茬的粗糙不平的绿色。迪格雷刚开始不知道是什么，直到其中一个来到离他很近的地方。那是一种长而尖的小东西，身上长出几十支手臂，上面班盖着绿色之物，而且以每两秒钟一寸的速度增大。现在他的周围到处都有这样的东西。等它们长到与他高度相似时，他才恍然大悟地喊道“树！”</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 早上好，保罗。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 嗨，早上好，你今天这么早。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 是啊，今天交通状况不错，所以我可以早点来公司。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 原来如此，你每天到公司要花多长时间？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 嗯，大约一个小时左右。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 很长的路程啊。你开车吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 不，我乘坐公共交通工具，这比较安全。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 你说的对，但是我起床较晚，那让我别无选择，只能骑摩托车。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Good morning, Paul.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Hi, good morning. You're so early today.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Yes, traffic wasn't much today, so I made it to the office earlier.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: I see. How long does it take you to reach the office everyday?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Well, about an hour or so.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: That's quite a long journey. Do you drive a car?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: No, I take public transportation. It's safer.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: You're right. But I get up a little late, that gives me no other option but to travel by motorcycle.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We returned home thoroughly contented.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们__________地回家了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">心满意足</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: data-w="400" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">→ credible adj. 可信的；可靠的</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Her excuse was barely <em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">credible</span></strong></em>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她的借口无法<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">让人信服</strong>。</p><p border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">credible</span></em></strong> explanation/witness</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">可信的</strong>解释╱证人</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">→ incredible</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">-in 否定前缀，<strong>incredible adj. 不可相信的，难以置信的</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">近义词：unbelievable</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><g style="box-sizing: border-box;">It’s</g><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><g style="box-sizing: border-box;">incredible </g></span></em></strong><g style="box-sizing: border-box;">that </g>he survived the fall.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他跌下去竟然能够生还，真<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">不可思议</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">And you are going to be an <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">incredible</span></em></strong> mother.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">而你也会是个<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">非常棒的</strong>母亲。</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: He met an <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">incredible</span></em></strong> woman.</p><p style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;text-align: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. irrational</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">→ rational adj.合理的；理性的；理智的</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">rational number 有理数</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">There is no <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">rational</span></em></strong> explanation for his actions.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对他的所作所为无法作出<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">合理的</strong>解释。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">→ irrational</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">-ir 否定前缀</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong>irrational adj. 不合理的，荒谬的</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">近义词：unreasonable</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He’s becoming increasingly <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">irrational</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他变得越来越<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">不可理喻</strong>了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He dismissed her fears as <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">irrational</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他认为她的恐惧<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">毫无道理</strong>而未加理睬。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I'm just trying to stop you from making <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">irrational</span></em></strong> choices.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我不想你<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">草率</strong>地做决定。</p></section><section style="z-index: 2;transform: translate(350.547px, 2888.73px);-webkit-transform: translate(350.547px, 2888.73px);-moz-transform: translate(350.547px, 2888.73px);-o-transform: translate(350.547px, 2888.73px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It's the <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">irrational</span></em></strong> fear that someone is after you…</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">总以为背后有人追赶的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">无端</strong>恐惧感。</p></section><section style="z-index: 2;transform: translate(350.547px, 3213.94px);-webkit-transform: translate(350.547px, 3213.94px);-moz-transform: translate(350.547px, data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKde9AMGibMHmvYPapYLicxJ3TO1mossIDKic0icmKzibYHh1sfnwjjydQUb0NqiaibrOG2Vsh6tbqVSUufwA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;">图片源自《绝望的主妇》</span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">3. obsessional adj. 痴迷的；迷恋的；耿耿于怀的</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链儿：be obsessional about XX  对XX痴迷</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">is obsessional about</span></em></strong> cleanliness.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她有洁癖。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She became almost <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">obsessional about</span></em></strong> the way she looked.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她关注自己的外表几乎接近<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">病态</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">→ obsess v.使痴迷，使迷恋，使心神不宁</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A lot of young girls are <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">obsessed </span></em></strong><g style="box-sizing: border-box;">by </g>their weight.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">许多年轻女孩都<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">过于担心</strong>自己的体重。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She's completely <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">obsessed</span></em></strong> with him.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他让她<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">神魂颠倒</strong>。<span style="text-align: center;font-size: 16px;"></span></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);text-align: left;margin: 20px 0% 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 40%;border-width: 0px 6px 0px 0px;border-style: solid;border-left-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);border-right-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);padding: 0px;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;background-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(252, 252, 252);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">   活学活用</em></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);padding: 0px 9px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">请用<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> be obsessional about XX </strong>随意造句</p></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(114, 114, 114);border-bottom-right-radius: 0px;padding: 0px 5px 4px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词汇补充</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;line-height: 1.2;padding-left: 3px;padding-right: 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Vocabulary</strong></p></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">请上下滑动查看</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: transparent;padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(17, 1, 1);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1. prefer to do 更喜欢;宁愿做;宁愿</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I'd prefer to reserve judgement until I know all the facts. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">在了解全部事实之前我不想发表意见。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2. earn money 挣钱;赚钱</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I used to earn money by mowing lawns. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我以前靠修剪草坪赚钱。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">3. wish 表示与现在/过去/将来事实相反或不太可能实现的愿望时，要用虚拟语气</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">现在--从句时态：动词过去式</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I wish I were a bird.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">真希望我是一只鸟啊。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">过去--从句时态：would(could, might) have ＋过去分词</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">或had ＋过去分词</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I wish I hadn't eaten so much. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我倒希望我没有吃这么多。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I wish I would have done better. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">真希望我能表现得再好一点。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">将来--从句时态：would(could, might)+动词原形</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I wish she would try again.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我希望她能再试一次</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">4. Shall </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ʃəl; strong ʃæl/ modal verb </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">(negative short form shan’t) (同I和we连用，表示将来)将要，将会;在疑问句中同I和we连用，表示提出或征求意见;(表示决心、命令或指示)必须，一定，应该</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Shall we go for plan A or plan B? </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们选用第一方案还是第二方案？</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;padding: 0px 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;margin-top: 1.15em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 6px;height: 6px;margin-top: -3px;border-radius: 100%;float: left;background-color: rgb(232, 181, 181);box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style="border-top: 1px solid rgb(232, 181, 181);width: 99.9%;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section style="text-align: right;margin: -1.1em 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);text-align: left;padding: 3px 10px;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">第三步   认真校对，查缺补漏</p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px;padding-left: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 95%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-left: 1px solid rgb(249, 110, 87);height: 1.2em;box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style='border-radius: 100%;margin-left: -0.8em;display: inline-block;float: left;width: 1.6em;height: 1.6em;background-position: center center;background-repeat: 0px 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="padding-bottom: 8px;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="clear: none;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">听写方法：</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">完成今天的任务了么？不！千万不要丢掉极其重要的一步：校对！</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有两个方面要校对：</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.没有听出来的意群：可能包括连读或者省音,分析错误的原因并做笔记。</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.没有听出来或听错的单词:每篇校对后写在听写笔记下面并罗列,这些才是你每天的进步之基。</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(188, 132, 37);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">今日听写答案</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;color: rgba(122, 120, 124, 0.91);font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">（请务必听写后校对） </span></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">红色连读</span><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">；<span style="color: rgba(46, 159, 238, 0.863);box-sizing: border-box;">蓝色爆破省读</span>；<span style="color: rgb(255, 129, 36);box-sizing: border-box;">橙色弱读 <span style="font-size: 14px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></span></span></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 17px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;">Wednesday</span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">‘In America, young ladies prefer to work an</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> earn money for themselves’, said Mr. Broo</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">ke</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> quickly, ‘an</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> not expect others to pay for everything.’</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">在美国，青年女子喜欢为自己工作挣钱，布鲁克先生很快接话，她们不指望别人给她们掏钱。</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">‘I see,’ said Miss Kate, coldly. Soo</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">n a</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">fter, she took her drawing an</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> move</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d a</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">way.</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">是这样，凯特小姐冷冷地说。没过一会儿，她拿起她的画走开了。</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">‘There’s no place like America for us workers, Miss Meg’, sai</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> Mr. Brooke, smiling.</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">没有其它地方像美国这样适合我们工作的人了，麦格小姐，布鲁克先生笑着说。</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">His brown eyes look</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ed a</span></span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> Meg warmly, and she smiled bac</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">k at </span></span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">h</span></span></span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">i</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">m.</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">他棕色的眼睛温和地看着麦格，她也向他笑笑。</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">‘I wish I liked teaching as mu</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ch a</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">s you do’, she said.</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">我真希望像你一样喜欢教书，她说。</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">‘You would if you were teaching Laurie’,said Mr. Brooke</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">．</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">‘I'll be sorry when he goes to college next year. But then I shall beco</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">me a</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> soldier.’</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">如果你教的是罗瑞，你就会喜欢教书的，布鲁克先生说，明年他要去上大学，我会感到很难过。不过之后我就要去当兵了。</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">‘I think every young man wants to be a soldier’, said Meg, ‘bu</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t i</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">t’s hard for the family who stay a</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t </span></span><span style="text-decoration: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">我认为每个年轻人都想成为一名军人，麦格说，可这对呆在家里的人来说是很难的。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">There was certainly plenty to watch and to listen to. The tree which Digory had noticed was now a full-grown beech whose branches swayed gently above his head. They stood on cool, green grass, sprinkled with daisies and buttercups. A little way off, along the river bank, willows were growing. On the other side tangles of flowering currant, lilac, wild rose, and rhododendron closed them in. The horse was tearing up delicious mouthfuls of new grass.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">值得看和值得听的实在太多了。迪格雷最先看见的那棵树己经长成一棵粗壮的山毛榉，枝丫优美地在他头顶上舒展。他们站立的那片凉爽的青草地上散布着雏菊和毛莨属植物。稍远的地方，沿河生长着柳树。河的对岸，绽放着一丛丛茶藨子、丁香花、野玫瑰和杜鹃花。那匹马大口大口地撕咬着新鲜的草。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 天哪，我有段时间没见你了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 是啊，我离开了两个月。很高兴再见到你，你近来怎么样？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 我很好，谢谢。你晒黑了，我看起来很健康，你这段时间去哪儿了？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 北戴河。我在那儿玩得很开心。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 你都干了什么？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 我每天都去游泳和跑步。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 真的吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 是啊，有时候我还会去爬山。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 真有意思，回头你得给我好好讲讲。能见到你真的很高兴，不过恐怕我得走了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 回头见。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Good heavens. I haven't seen you for some time.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Yeah. I've been away for the past two months. Good to see you again, how have you been?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Very well, thanks. And you're looking brown and healthy. Where have you been?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Beidaihe. I had a wonderful time there.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Oh, what did you do exactly?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: I went swimming and jogging everyday.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Really?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Yes. And sometimes I went climbing.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: How interesting. You must tell me all about it later. It's really nice to see you again. I'm afraid I have to go now.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: See you later.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You don't ___________ anything but yourself and your precious face.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你什么都不关心，除了你自己和你那张娇贵的脸。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">care about</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: 你永远也不知道前方会发生什么。</strong></p></section></section></section><section style="z-index: 101;transform: translate(357px, 289.531px);-webkit-transform: translate(357px, 289.531px);-moz-transform: 连读同化：</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong>don'<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);text-decoration: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. 词链儿：don't you ever do </strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><g style="box-sizing: border-box;">something  </g></strong></p><p style="font-weight: 400;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><g style="box-sizing: border-box;">不要</g></strong><strong border-box;"/></p><p style="font-weight: 400;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="font-weight: 400;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing:
