border-box;">again.</g></p><p style="font-weight: 400;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">不要</strong>再<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">碰</strong>我了。</p><p style="font-weight: 400;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="font-weight: 400;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. 词链儿：look behind you 向后看</strong></p><p style="font-weight: 400;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="font-weight: 400;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">相反：look ahead of you 向前看</strong></p><p style="font-weight: 400;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="font-weight: 400;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">3. There's nothing for you behind you. </strong></p><p style="font-weight: 400;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: All that exists is what's ahead. </strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong>所有东西都在前方。</strong></p><p style="font-weight: 400;white-space: 1.8;letter-spacing: 1px;padding: 0px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(250, 224, 74);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"># </strong></span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">地道表达：</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">欣然接受XX  take kindly to sth</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She does <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">not </span><span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">take kindly to</span> criticism (=reacts badly to criticism).</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她<em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">不乐于接受</span></em>批评。</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">在这里，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">take的含义是：</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> 〔以某种方式〕处理，理解，考虑</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I was joking, but he <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">took </span>me seriously.</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我是在开玩笑，但他却<em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">当</span></em>真了。</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;">提醒：越是这种高频的小词，往往用法越是多种多样，而且非常好用。大家可以自行查一下take相关的词条，整理下来，一定会收货颇丰。</span></em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">night ˈnight</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">（儿童用语或对儿童使用的语言）晚安</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> ‘<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">Night night</span>, sleep tight!’</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">Good night</span>. Sleep well.</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">非正式场合，也可以直接说“Night.”</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(250, 224, 74);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"># </strong></span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">地道表达：</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我就不留你了。这句在日常待人接客中常用的客套话，你会怎么说呢？</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">影片中使用：convince一词：</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">convince sb to do sth 就等于 <br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">persuade sb to do sth</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">说服，劝服某人做某事。</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I can't convince you to stay. </p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我就不劝你留下了/我就不留你了...</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section><section center;margin: 0px 0% 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.5305556" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/L4LJPfaSIKdpRko4UicdJ2BSy977ibTGRfouDGJVmaLpicHibJd9QvYTmIKuw0wjfhzVjVERmuYFjiaYD6rs4cFiaRDA/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 1px;padding: 0px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(250, 224, 74);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"># </strong></span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">地道表达：</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">爱上某人，是不是第一个出现在脑海中的表达就是：fall in love with sb ？</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">咱们再学个表达：</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">be taken with/by sth/sb </strong></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">字面含义，被...带走了。什么样的情况下我们会被带走呢？自然是某物/某人非常attractive or interesting。因此这个表达的含义也就是：被…吸引；迷上；对…感兴趣</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">were all very taken with</span> his girlfriend. 我们都觉得他的女朋友<em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">非常讨人喜欢</span></em>。</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;">（嗯，还是别人的女朋友好。</span></em><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;">好扎心有木有！）</span></em></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/L4LJPfaSIKdpRko4UicdJ2BSy977ibTGRfOjrHRSxbOxfrEsHYKc4SB7kYzPvRKljnlCKicIm3Kn9soJgHunYrhmA/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: 1.8;letter-spacing: 1px;padding: 0px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(250, 224, 74);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"># </strong></span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">地道表达：</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">欣然接受XX  take kindly to sth</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She does <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">not </span><span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">take kindly to</span> criticism (=reacts badly to criticism).</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她<em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">不乐于接受</span></em>批评。</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">在这里，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">take的含义是：</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> 〔以某种方式〕处理，理解，考虑</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I was joking, but he <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">took </span>me seriously.</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我是在开玩笑，但他却<em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">当</span></em>真了。</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;">提醒：越是这种高频的小词，往往用法越是多种多样，而且非常好用。大家可以自行查一下take相关的词条，整理下来，一定会收货颇丰。</span></em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">非正式场合，也可以直接说“Night.”</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我就不留你了。这句在日常待人接客中常用的客套话，你会怎么说呢？</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">影片中使用：convince一词：</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">convince sb to do sth 就等于 <br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">persuade sb to do sth</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">说服，劝服某人做某事。</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I can't convince you to stay. </p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我就不劝你留下了/我就不留你了...</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section><section 62);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 0px 0% 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.5305556" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/L4LJPfaSIKdpRko4UicdJ2BSy977ibTGRfouDGJVmaLpicHibJd9QvYTmIKuw0wjfhzVjVERmuYFjiaYD6rs4cFiaRDA/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 1px;padding: 0px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(250, 224, 74);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"># </strong></span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">地道表达：</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">爱上某人，是不是第一个出现在脑海中的表达就是：fall in love with sb ？</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">咱们再学个表达：</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">be taken with/by sth/sb </strong></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">字面含义，被...带走了。什么样的情况下我们会被带走呢？自然是某物/某人非常attractive or interesting。因此这个表达的含义也就是：被…吸引；迷上；对…感兴趣</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">were all very taken with</span> his girlfriend. 我们都觉得他的女朋友<em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">非常讨人喜欢</span></em>。</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;">（嗯，还是别人的女朋友好。</span></em><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;">好扎心有木有！）</span></em></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">请上下滑动查看</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: transparent;padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(17, 1, 1);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">cheer up </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：to become more cheerful; to make sb/sth more cheerful</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">中文释义：（使）变得更高兴，振奋起来</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Oh, come on—cheer up! 噢，得了，高兴起来吧！</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Give Mary a call; she needs cheering up. 给玛丽打个电话，她需要人安慰。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Bright curtains can cheer up a dull room. 色彩鲜艳的窗帘可以让单调的房间变得亮丽起来。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">amusement </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">音标：/ əˈmjuːzmənt /  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：the feeling that you have when sth is funny or amusing, or it entertains you </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">中文释义：可笑；愉悦；娱乐</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She could not hide her amusement at the way he was dancing. 她见他跳舞的姿势，不禁笑出声来。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">To my amusement he couldn't get the door open. 使我感到好笑的是，他竟然打不开门。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Her eyes twinkled with amusement. 她的眼睛闪耀着愉悦的光芒。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;padding: 0px 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;margin-top: 1.15em;box-sizing: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">她这样反复了好几次，使得在街对面看着她的一个年轻人感到很有意思。</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">But the fourth time</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">，</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">Jo ga</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ve<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"> h</span>er</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">sel</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">f a</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> shake and walked up the stairs</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">．</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">可是第四次，琼鼓了鼓勇气，走上了楼梯。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">All this time the Lion's song, and his stately prowl, to and fro, backwards and forwards, was going on. What was rather alarming was that at each turn he came a little nearer. Polly was finding the song more and more interesting because she thought she was beginning to see the connection between the music and the things that were happening. When a line of dark firs sprang up on a ridge about a hundred yards away she felt that they were connected with a series of deep, prolonged notes which the Lion had sung a second before. And when he burst into a rapid series of lighter notes she was not surprised to see primroses suddenly appearing in every direction. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">在这段时间里，狮子一直不停地唱着歌，庄严地前后左右走动。使人惊异的是，它每次转身，都离他们更近一些。波莉发现，歌声越来越有趣，因为她觉得自己开始看出了音乐与眼前发生的事之间的联系。当大约百米外的山脊上跳出一排墨绿色的冷杉树时，她感到这和一秒钟前狮子唱的一组低沉、悠长的音调紧密相关。豪不奇怪，随着狮了唱出一组轻快的旋律，她看到报春花从四面八方长了出来。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 朱莉娅晚上有空吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 什么事？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 想约你一块儿去看电影。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 你是想和我约会吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 是的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 我不喜欢在电影院约会，那里太吵。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 你想在哪儿见面？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 我们去咖啡店吧，那里很安静。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 我们几点见面？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 七点怎么样？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 好的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Julia, are you free tonight?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: What's up?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: I want to invite you to go to the movies.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Are you asking me for a date?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Yes.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: I don't like to go to the movies on a date. It's noisy there.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Where do you want to meet?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Let's go to the coffee shop then. It's quiet there.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: What time should we meet?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: How about seven?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: All right.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Remember that when both of you were in need, I was the one who_______________.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">记住，在你们两个都有困难的时候，是我借钱给你们的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">loaned you money</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">今日发音练习重点：</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong>1. mortal 中第二音节发音方法为舌边爆破或弹舌音+舌侧音； </strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong>2. ac‧cu‧mu‧late  /əˈkjuːmjəleɪt, əˈkjuːmjʊleɪt/ 包含四音节，重在第二音节。</strong></p></section><section style="z-index: 2;transform: translate(350.547px, border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">言之有物</em></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. mortal love 凡人之爱</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">mortal adj. 不能永生的；终将死亡的；凡人的</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We are all <em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">mortal</span></strong></em>. 我们都<strong>终</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">有一死</strong>。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">mortal n. 凡人；普通人</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="text-align: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">E</strong>: Cool. I work for the firm that reps Pierre. Have you guys ever considered <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">taking on</strong> a team? You're growing so fast, I imagine <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">you're not as hands-on as you'd like</strong>.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">G</strong>: Well, we<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> do our marketing in-house</strong>. And we manage to<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> stay pretty hands-on</strong>, but thanks.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">J</strong>: Damn, we have a problem.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">E</strong>: What...what is it?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">J</strong>: There are thunderstorms in Dallas.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">E</strong>: Why is that a problem?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">J</strong>: Well, Amanda and Frank Carrouth's plane got delayed. She was supposed to wear the dress, and her oil-billionaire husband promised he'd <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">bid on it</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">E</strong>: Merde.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">M</strong>: Well, that doesn't sound too good.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">E</strong>: No, everything's fine. We just kind of lost our model. Judith, this is Mathieu Cadault. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">J:</strong> I know who he is. Pleasure, hon. You must <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">have a dozen models on speed dial</strong> we could <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">ask for a last-minute favor</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">M</strong>: What's going on?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">J</strong>: We need someone to wear Pierre's dress for the auction.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">M</strong>: I have the perfect person.</p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: 1.1;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">情景解读</strong></p></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: auto;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;height: auto;align-self: flex-end;line-height: 0;letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;justify-content: flex-start;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style='display: inline-block;width: 30px;height: 20px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;line-height: 0;letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(0, 120, 223);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Emily在聚会上碰到了前卫设计师组合。Emily立刻变身工作狂，询问他们是否需要雇佣营销公司为他们做市场营销。然而，设计师却婉拒了Emily,说他们目前在自己做营销，并且还能应付过来。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;justify-content: center;margin: 10px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: auto;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;height: auto;align-self: flex-end;line-height: 0;letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: right;justify-content: flex-end;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style='display: inline-block;width: 40px;height: 20px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;background-image: url("https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/GjnjEuOE1jJwpenIuLv1Hn6Qqibx5kqT5NXJz2xfSd5kl21TKSmOZEpBLR3XgSXDetAZS6MhRLfqI672HH3bbrA/640?wx_fmt=png");background-position: 50% 50%;background-repeat: 1.1;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链精解</strong></p></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: auto;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;height: auto;align-self: flex-end;line-height: 0;letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;justify-content: flex-start;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style='display: inline-block;width: 30px;height: 20px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;background-image: url("https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/JZLztib6YXpkKEPo1gaxIVeltBica08RfFqoSXsWd5oDeYYciawW5DibnzFATQwx1S7Cc6otz64IniabDK2WDMMAuUg/640?wx_fmt=png");background-position: 50% 50%;background-repeat: no-repeat;background-size: contain;background-attachment: scroll;box-sizing: border-box;'></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;justify-content: center;margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 75px;height: 16px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;line-height: 0;letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(0, 120, 223);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">大家在视频里找到今天的主题表达了吗？<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">原句1</strong>：You're growing so fast, I imagine you're not <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">as hands-on as you'd like</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">原句2：</strong>Well, we do our marketing in-house. And we manage to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">stay pretty hands-on</strong>, but thanks.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">hands-on 在这里就是亲力亲为；事必躬亲的；实际操作意思。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句1</strong>：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> I'll have a <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">hands-on </strong>computer training tonight. 我今晚有个计算机<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">操作</strong>培训。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句2</strong>：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He works hard to gain <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">hands-on </strong>experience of industry. 他努力工作以获得<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">实际经验</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句3：</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She has a <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">hands-on</strong> style of management. 她在管理方面<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">事必躬亲</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">从这两个原句中，我们还可以学到两个词链。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;">be not as hands-on as XX would like 应付不过来</span></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：As a mother who has three kids, you are not<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> as hands-on as you'd like about housework</strong>. 作为三个孩子的妈妈，肯定有些家务<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">应付不过来</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">manage to stay pretty hands-on 应付得过来。</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：As a new mother, I manage to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">stay pretty hands-on</strong> about taking care of a baby. 作为新手妈妈，照顾孩子我还<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">应付得过来</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;justify-content: center;margin: 10px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: We just kind of lost our model. Judith, this is Mathieu Cadault. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">J:</strong> I know who he is. Pleasure, hon. You must <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">have a dozen models on speed dial</strong> we could <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">ask for a last-minute favor</strong>.</p><p border-box;">Emily在聚会上碰到了前卫设计师组合。Emily立刻变身工作狂，询问他们是否需要雇佣营销公司为他们做市场营销。然而，设计师却婉拒了Emily,说他们目前在自己做营销，并且还能应付过来。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p 1.1;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链精解</strong></p></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: auto;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;height: auto;align-self: flex-end;line-height: 0;letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;justify-content: flex-start;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style='display: inline-block;width: 30px;height: 20px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;background-image: url("https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/JZLztib6YXpkKEPo1gaxIVeltBica08RfFqoSXsWd5oDeYYciawW5DibnzFATQwx1S7Cc6otz64IniabDK2WDMMAuUg/640?wx_fmt=png");background-position: 50% 50%;background-repeat: no-repeat;background-size: contain;background-attachment: scroll;box-sizing: border-box;'></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;justify-content: center;margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 75px;height: 16px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;line-height: 0;letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(0, 120, 223);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">大家在视频里找到今天的主题表达了吗？<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">原句1</strong>：You're growing so fast, I imagine you're not <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">as hands-on as you'd like</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">原句2：</strong>Well, we do our marketing in-house. And we manage to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">stay pretty hands-on</strong>, but thanks.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">hands-on 在这里就是亲力亲为；事必躬亲的；实际操作意思。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句1</strong>：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> I'll have a <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">hands-on </strong>computer training tonight. 我今晚有个计算机<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">操作</strong>培训。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句2</strong>：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He works hard to gain <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">hands-on </strong>experience of industry. 他努力工作以获得<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">实际经验</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句3：</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She has a <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">hands-on</strong> style of management. 她在管理方面<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">事必躬亲</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">从这两个原句中，我们还可以学到两个词链。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;">be not as hands-on as XX would like 应付不过来</span></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：As a mother who has three kids, you are not<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> as hands-on as you'd like about housework</strong>. 作为三个孩子的妈妈，肯定有些家务<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">应付不过来</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">manage to stay pretty hands-on 应付得过来。</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：As a new mother, I manage to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">stay pretty hands-on</strong> about taking care of a baby. 作为新手妈妈，照顾孩子我还<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">应付得过来</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;justify-content: center;margin: 10px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: right;justify-content: flex-end;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style='display: inline-block;width: 40px;height: 20px;vertical-align: top;overflow: border-box;">自己做XX，不外包</strong></p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(0, 120, 223);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">原句：</strong>Well, we<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> do our marketing in-house</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链</strong>：do XX in-house</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：I prefer to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">do</strong> that project<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> in-house.</strong> 我更希望我们<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">自己做</strong>这个项目。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: flex;flex-flow: row 0 auto;height: auto;align-self: flex-start;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;margin: 10px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: auto;align-self: flex-end;flex: 0 0 auto;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;height: auto;margin: 0px -10px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;transform: matrix(1, 0, -0.2, 1, 0, 0);-webkit-transform: matrix(1, 0, -0.2, 1, 0, 0);-moz-transform: matrix(1, 0, -0.2, 1, 0, 0);-o-transform: matrix(1, 0, -0.2, 1, 0, 0);border-style: none;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 0px style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;border-top: 0px none rgb(62, 62, 62);border-top-left-radius: 10px;overflow: hidden;background-image: linear-gradient(315deg, rgb(34, 163, powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, style="display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: auto;vertical-align: bottom;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 0px 0px 10px;border-style: border-box;"><section style="text-align: left;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(0, 120, 223);letter-spacing: 2px;line-height: 1;padding: 0px 20px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">have XX on speed dial </strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">可以马上把XX找来;可以联络上XX</strong></p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(0, 120, 223);box-sizing: border-box;">原句：</span></strong><span style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(0, 120, 223);box-sizing: border-box;">You must <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">have a dozen models on speed dial </strong>we could ask for a last-minute favor.</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(0, 120, 223);box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(0, 120, 223);box-sizing: border-box;"> 词链：</span></strong><span style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(0, 120, 223);box-sizing: border-box;">have XX on speed dial</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(0, 120, 223);box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(0, 120, 223);box-sizing: border-box;">将某人的手机号码设置为快速拨号模式，一定是跟这个人非常熟悉，经常联系。所以这个词链就引申为：可以马上找到XX；可以联络上XX的意思啦。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(0, 120, 223);box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(0, 120, 223);box-sizing: border-box;">例句</span></strong><span style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(0, 120, 223);box-sizing: border-box;">：You must<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> have some doctors on speed dial </strong>as a mother. Because you don't know when your kids would feel bad. 作为母亲，你得能<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">马上联系到</strong>一些医生。因为你不知道你的孩子什么时候就会不舒服。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(0, 120, 223);box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p></section><section 40);box-sizing: border-box;">马奇小姐，著名的美国作家！</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">”</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">罗瑞说道，边说边把他的帽子扔到空中，然后又接住。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Thus, with an unspeakable thrill, she felt quite certain that all the things were coming (as she said) "out of the Lion's head". When you listened to his song you heard the things he was making up: when you looked round you, you saw them. This was so exciting that she had no time to be afraid. But Digory and the Cabby could not help feeling a bit nervous as each turn of the Lion's walk brought him nearer. As for Uncle Andrew, his teeth were chattering, but his knees were shaking so that he could not run away.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">在一阵无以言表的激动中，她肯定所有这些都是从（用她的话说） “狮子脑袋里出来的”。当你聆听它歌唱时，你就听见了它所创造的事物：当你环顾四周，你就能看见这些事物。这太令人激动了，她无暇感到害怕。但狮子每一次转身离他们更近时，迪格雷和马车夫都不禁有些紧张，安德鲁舅舅则牙齿打战，双膝发抖，根本跑不掉了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 麻烦问一下，我怎样才能得到特价的优惠券？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 买的多就多送特价优惠券。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 如果买这些东西，我能得到一张减价的优惠券吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 当然可以了，每买三袋糖就可以获得一张优惠券。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 但是如果我下次用它去买东西会优惠多少呢？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 凭此券可优惠10便士。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 我可以用它买超市里的任何东西吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 是呀，你需要在过期之前把它用了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 优惠券多长时间内有效啊？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 一年内都可以用。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 我明白了，我要买9袋糖，也就是可以得到3张购物券了吧。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 好的，我帮你拿。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Excuse me, how can I get special discount coupons?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Buy more and get more special discount coupons.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Can I get a discount coupon if I buy these goods?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Of course. You get a coupon for every 3 bags of sugar.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: But how much discount can I get if I use it to buy goods next time?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 10 pence off if you use this coupon.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Can I buy everything in a supermarket by it?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Yeah. You need to take advantage of it within its expiry date.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: How long can I keep it?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: The coupon can be used at least one year.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: I see. I will take 9 bags of sugar so that I can get 3 coupons.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: All right. I'll get them for you.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">This realization of our dreams __________ even our wildest expectations.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们梦想的实现甚至超越了我们最大胆的估计.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">surpassed</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><p style="text-align: center;"><strong style='max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Helvetica Neue", "PingFang SC", "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei UI", "Microsoft YaHei", normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A /dʒ/  B /ʒ/  C /tʃ/</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><a data-itemshowtype="0" data-linktype="2" border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">A 对</strong>  B 错</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;line-height: 2;letter-spacing: 0px;color: rgb(9, 9, 9);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Hi there.你好</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">One sec. Could you hold on for a moment? </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">抱歉，请等我一下。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We'd love a table for two. -The name?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">- 两个人用餐-请问贵姓？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We don't... We don't have a reservation.我们没订位。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I'm sorry, sir, we're booked until October.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">抱歉，都客满了订位到十月。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">October? 十月？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Well...好吧。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">l'll get back to you.再联络。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">That went well.可真顺利。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It's no big deal.又没什么大不了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Oh, come on, stop it.别难过了啦。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It's the best restaurant in town. Nobody gets a table here.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这是全市最好的餐厅没订位进不去。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">No, it's not that. -Well, what is it?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">-不是为了这件事。-不然呢？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I didn't do this right.我没做对。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">There wasn't a meeting. -You'd see me if there was no big deal.-你不是来开会吧？-没特别的事你才会见我。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">If it was just... -Ambush.-如果只是…-你算计我。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">...you know, coffee, and coffee can turn into dinner...只是喝咖啡喝完咖啡吃晚饭……</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">...dinner can turn into... -Turn into what?-吃完晚饭…-怎样？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I do sometimes get a few steps ahead of myself.我承认有时候会猴急抢个几步。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Morgan, a few steps? 几步？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You're always leaping 10 steps ahead.你每次都抢先至少十步。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We were dating, what, a week? 我们才交往，一个礼拜？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">And you had our entire future mapped out for us? 你就规划好我们整个未来？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1________________________________.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I'd go to your house you'd have the entire town in your house to meet me. 我才去你家度个周末你就邀请所有的朋友给我认识。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2_________________________________.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">What are you talking about? 你在胡说什么？ </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You know what I'm talking about.你心里有数。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">That guy. -What guy?-就那个男人啊。-什么男人？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The guy I caught you making out with. -I wasn't making out with him.-被我逮到和你热吻的那家伙。-我没和他热吻。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">What, are we in junior high school right now? 我们又不是中学生了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">What do you call it, then? 不然那是怎样？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A kiss.亲一下而已。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It was just one kiss with some random guy that just...只是和某个男人随意亲了一下。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Years... You know what?好几年前的…你知道吗？</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="height: 100%;width:
